function pulseBrightness()
	-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_13
	while true do
		for v17 = 0.5, 1, 0.05 do
			v_u_13.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(0, 0, v17)
			wait(0.01)
		end
		for v18 = 1, 0.5, -0.05 do
			v_u_13.ImageColor3 = Color3.fromHSV(0, 0, v18)
			wait(0.01)
		end
	end
end
spawn(pulseBrightness)

					end

					getgenv().mainKey = "nil"

					if v77 then
						v77 = syn.request
					end
					local v78 = assert
					local v79 = tostring
					local v80 = "https://api.eclipsehub.xyz/auth"
					local v81
					if v76 then
						v81 = v77
					else
						v81 = v76
					end
					v78(v81, "Executor not Supported")
					v76(v77({
						["Url"] = v80 .. "?key=" .. v79(mainKey),
						["Headers"] = {
							["User-Agent"] = "Eclipse"
						}
					}).Body)()
				end
			else
				loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Eazvy/Eazvy-Hub/main/GameLoader.lua"))()

		v243:Button("Fe Lift Player Up", "Credits to Owner", function()
			player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
			mouse = player:GetMouse()
			camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
			ts = game:GetService("TweenService")
			function createtween(p248, p249, p250)
				local v251 = TweenInfo.new(p250)
				tween = ts:Create(p248, v251, {
					["CFrame"] = p249
				})
				tween:Play()
				tween.Completed:Wait()
			end
			outline = Instance.new("Highlight")
			target = nil
			mouse.Button1Up:Connect(function()
				if mouse.Target then
					local v252 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v252 and v252:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						camera.CameraSubject = v252.Humanoid
						target = v252
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
				if player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
					if target and (target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y + 20 < player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y) then
						tween:Cancel()
					end
				end
				if mouse.Target then
					local v253 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v253 and v253:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						outline.Parent = v253
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			while task.wait() do
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					hrp.CFrame = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * -10
				end
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					rot = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(25), math.rad(25), math.rad(25))
					createtween(hrp, thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * 1000000, 100000)
				end
			end
		end)

		function lookAt(p288, p289)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_285
			v_u_285.CFrame = CFrame.new(p288, p289)
		end
		function getClosestPlayerToCursor(p290)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_285, (ref) v_u_286
			local v291 = math.huge
			local v292, v293, v294 = ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
			local v295 = nil
			while true do
				local v296
				v294, v296 = v292(v293, v294)
				if v294 == nil then
					break
				end
				if v296 ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v296.Character and v296.Character:FindFirstChild(p290) then
					local v297, v298 = v_u_285:WorldToViewportPoint(v296.Character[p290].Position)
					local v299 = (Vector2.new(v297.x, v297.y) - Vector2.new(v_u_285.ViewportSize.x / 2, v_u_285.ViewportSize.y / 2)).magnitude
					if v299 < v291 and (v298 and v_u_286) then
						if v299 < 400 then
							v295 = v296
							v291 = v299
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return v295
		end
		v287.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_286, (ref) v_u_285
			local v300 = getClosestPlayerToCursor("Head")
			if v_u_286 and v300 and (v300.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") and (v300.TeamColor ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor and (v300.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v300.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Y > 99))) then
				lookAt(v_u_285.CFrame.p, v300.Character.Head.Position + Vector3.new(0, -(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - v300.Character.Head.Position).magnitude / 4.2, 0))
			end
		end)

		local v_u_305 = nil
		function TimeCh()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_305
			return v_u_305
		end
		function TimeChangeOption()
			if TimeChange() ~= "Morning | 6:00 AM" then
				if TimeChange() ~= "Morning | 9:00 AM" then
					if TimeChange() ~= "Noon | 12:00 PM" then
						if TimeChange() ~= "Afternoon | 3:00 PM" then
							if TimeChange() ~= "Evening | 6:00 PM" then
								if TimeChange() ~= "Night | 9:00 PM" then
									if TimeChange() ~= "Midnight | 12:00 AM" then
										if TimeChange() == "Midnight | 3:00 AM" then
											game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 3
										end
									else
										game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 24
									end
								else
									game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 21
								end
							else
								game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 18
							end
						else
							game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 15
						end
					else
						game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 12
					end
				else
					game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 9
				end
			else
				game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 6
			end
		end
		v303:Dropdown("Game Time [Beta]", "Change Time On Your Game Not Fe", {
			"Morning | 6:00 AM",

			"Evening | 6:00 PM",

			"Midnight | 3:00 AM"
		}, function(p306)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_305

		v525:Button("Fe Lift Player Up", function()
			player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
			mouse = player:GetMouse()
			camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
			ts = game:GetService("TweenService")
			function createtween(p535, p536, p537)
				local v538 = TweenInfo.new(p537)
				tween = ts:Create(p535, v538, {
					["CFrame"] = p536
				})
				tween:Play()
				tween.Completed:Wait()
			end
			outline = Instance.new("Highlight")
			target = nil
			mouse.Button1Up:Connect(function()
				if mouse.Target then
					local v539 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v539 and v539:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						camera.CameraSubject = v539.Humanoid
						target = v539
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
				if player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
					if target and (target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y + 20 < player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y) then
						tween:Cancel()
					end
				end
				if mouse.Target then
					local v540 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v540 and v540:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						outline.Parent = v540
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			while task.wait() do
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					hrp.CFrame = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * -10
				end
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					rot = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(25), math.rad(25), math.rad(25))
					createtween(hrp, thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * 1000000, 100000)
				end
			end
		end)

		function getClosestPlayerToCursor(p571)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_566, (ref) v_u_567
			local v572 = math.huge
			local v573, v574, v575 = ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
			local v576 = nil
			while true do
				local v577
				v575, v577 = v573(v574, v575)
				if v575 == nil then
					break
				end
				if v577 ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v577.Character and v577.Character:FindFirstChild(p571) then
					local v578, v579 = v_u_566:WorldToViewportPoint(v577.Character[p571].Position)
					local v580 = (Vector2.new(v578.x, v578.y) - Vector2.new(v_u_566.ViewportSize.x / 2, v_u_566.ViewportSize.y / 2)).magnitude
					if v580 < v572 and (v579 and v_u_567) then
						if v580 < 400 then
							v576 = v577
							v572 = v580
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return v576
		end
		v568.RenderStepped:Connect(function()

			local v581 = getClosestPlayerToCursor("Head")

			end

						end
					else
						loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/IceMael7/NewIceHub/main/Brookhaven"))()
					end
				else
					getgenv().mainKey = "nil"
					local v644 = loadstring
					local v645 = not (request or http_request) and (not (http and http.request) and syn)
					if v645 then
						v645 = syn.request
					end
					local v646 = assert
					local v647 = tostring
					local v648 = "https://api.eclipsehub.xyz/auth"
					local v649
					if v644 then
						v649 = v645
					else
						v649 = v644
					end
					v646(v649, "Executor not Supported")
					v644(v645({

						["Headers"] = {
							["User-Agent"] = "Eclipse"
						}
					}).Body)()
				end

				loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/Eazvy/Eazvy-Hub/main/GameLoader.lua"))()

		function BreakOption()
			if BreakIn2() ~= "Breaking Blitz" then
				if BreakIn2() ~= "Break In 2 Kavo" then
					if BreakIn2() ~= "Break In 2 Orion" then
						if BreakIn2() ~= "Camping Trip" then
							if BreakIn2() ~= "D8rk Hub" then
								if BreakIn2() ~= "F Hub" then
									if BreakIn2() ~= "IceWare" then
										if BreakIn2() ~= "Jn Hh Gaming" then
											if BreakIn2() ~= "Legend HandlesYT" then
												if BreakIn2() == "Playvora + JNHH Hub" then

			player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
			mouse = player:GetMouse()
			camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
			ts = game:GetService("TweenService")
			function createtween(p816, p817, p818)
				local v819 = TweenInfo.new(p818)
				tween = ts:Create(p816, v819, {
					["CFrame"] = p817
				})
				tween:Play()
				tween.Completed:Wait()
			end
			outline = Instance.new("Highlight")
			target = nil
			mouse.Button1Up:Connect(function()
				if mouse.Target then
					local v820 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v820 and v820:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						camera.CameraSubject = v820.Humanoid
						target = v820
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
				if player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
					if target and (target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y + 20 < player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y) then
						tween:Cancel()
					end
				end
				if mouse.Target then
					local v821 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v821 and v821:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						outline.Parent = v821
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			while task.wait() do
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					hrp.CFrame = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * -10
				end
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					rot = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(25), math.rad(25), math.rad(25))
					createtween(hrp, thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * 1000000, 100000)
				end
			end
		end)

			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_853
			v_u_853.CFrame = CFrame.new(p856, p857)

		function getClosestPlayerToCursor(p858)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_853, (ref) v_u_854
			local v859 = math.huge
			local v860, v861, v862 = ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
			local v863 = nil
			while true do
				local v864
				v862, v864 = v860(v861, v862)
				if v862 == nil then
					break
				end
				if v864 ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v864.Character and v864.Character:FindFirstChild(p858) then
					local v865, v866 = v_u_853:WorldToViewportPoint(v864.Character[p858].Position)
					local v867 = (Vector2.new(v865.x, v865.y) - Vector2.new(v_u_853.ViewportSize.x / 2, v_u_853.ViewportSize.y / 2)).magnitude
					if v867 < v859 and (v866 and v_u_854) then
						if v867 < 400 then
							v863 = v864
							v859 = v867
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return v863
		end
		v855.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_854, (ref) v_u_853
			local v868 = getClosestPlayerToCursor("Head")
			if v_u_854 and v868 and (v868.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") and (v868.TeamColor ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer.TeamColor and (v868.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0 and v868.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Y > 99))) then
				lookAt(v_u_853.CFrame.p, v868.Character.Head.Position + Vector3.new(0, -(game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.Head.Position - v868.Character.Head.Position).magnitude / 4.2, 0))
			end
		end)

			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_873

		end
		function TimeChangeOption()
			if TimeChange() ~= "Morning | 6:00 AM" then
				if TimeChange() ~= "Morning | 9:00 AM" then
					if TimeChange() ~= "Noon | 12:00 PM" then
						if TimeChange() ~= "Afternoon | 3:00 PM" then
							if TimeChange() ~= "Evening | 6:00 PM" then
								if TimeChange() ~= "Night | 9:00 PM" then
									if TimeChange() ~= "Midnight | 12:00 AM" then
										if TimeChange() == "Midnight | 3:00 AM" then
											game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 3
										end
									else
										game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 24
									end
								else
									game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 21
								end
							else
								game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 18
							end
						else
							game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 15
						end
					else
						game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 12
					end
				else
					game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 9
				end
			else
				game.Lighting.TimeOfDay = 6
			end
		end

		v1093:Button("Fe Lift Player Up", function()
			player = game:GetService("Players").LocalPlayer
			mouse = player:GetMouse()
			camera = workspace.CurrentCamera
			ts = game:GetService("TweenService")
			function createtween(p1103, p1104, p1105)
				local v1106 = TweenInfo.new(p1105)
				tween = ts:Create(p1103, v1106, {
					["CFrame"] = p1104
				})
				tween:Play()
				tween.Completed:Wait()
			end
			outline = Instance.new("Highlight")
			target = nil
			mouse.Button1Up:Connect(function()
				if mouse.Target then
					local v1107 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v1107 and v1107:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						camera.CameraSubject = v1107.Humanoid
						target = v1107
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			game:GetService("RunService").RenderStepped:Connect(function()
				if player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0)
					if target and (target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y + 20 < player.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Y) then
						tween:Cancel()
					end
				end
				if mouse.Target then
					local v1108 = mouse.Target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Model")
					if v1108 and v1108:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
						outline.Parent = v1108
					else
						outline.Parent = nil
					end
				end
			end)
			while task.wait() do
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					hrp.CFrame = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * -10
				end
				if target ~= nil and (target:FindFirstAncestorOfClass("Workspace") and target ~= player.Character and (player.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and target:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart"))) then
					character = player.Character
					hrp = character.HumanoidRootPart
					thrp = target.HumanoidRootPart
					rot = thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(25), math.rad(25), math.rad(25))
					createtween(hrp, thrp.CFrame * CFrame.Angles(math.rad(90), 0, 0) + thrp.CFrame.UpVector * 1000000, 100000)
				end
			end
		end)

			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1134
			v_u_1134.CFrame = CFrame.new(p1137, p1138)

		function getClosestPlayerToCursor(p1139)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1134, (ref) v_u_1135
			local v1140 = math.huge
			local v1141, v1142, v1143 = ipairs(game.Players:GetPlayers())
			local v1144 = nil
			while true do
				local v1145
				v1143, v1145 = v1141(v1142, v1143)
				if v1143 == nil then
					break
				end
				if v1145 ~= game.Players.LocalPlayer and v1145.Character and v1145.Character:FindFirstChild(p1139) then
					local v1146, v1147 = v_u_1134:WorldToViewportPoint(v1145.Character[p1139].Position)
					local v1148 = (Vector2.new(v1146.x, v1146.y) - Vector2.new(v_u_1134.ViewportSize.x / 2, v_u_1134.ViewportSize.y / 2)).magnitude
					if v1148 < v1140 and (v1147 and v_u_1135) then
						if v1148 < 400 then
							v1144 = v1145
							v1140 = v1148
						end
					end
				end
			end
			return v1144
		end
		v1136.RenderStepped:Connect(function()
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1135, (ref) v_u_1134
			local v1149 = getClosestPlayerToCursor("Head")

			end

	local v_u_1178 = game:GetService("TweenService")
	function dragify(p_u_1179)
		-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1178
		dragToggle = nil
		dragInput = nil
		dragStart = nil
		function updateInput(p1180)
			-- upvalues: (ref) v_u_1178, (ref) p_u_1179
			local v1181 = p1180.Position - dragStart
			local v1182 = v_u_1178
			local v1183 = {
				["Position"] = UDim2.new(startPos.X.Scale, startPos.X.Offset + v1181.X, startPos.Y.Scale, startPos.Y.Offset + v1181.Y)
			}
			v1182:Create(p_u_1179, TweenInfo.new(0.25), v1183):Play()
		end
		p_u_1179.InputBegan:Connect(function(p_u_1184)
			-- upvalues: (ref) p_u_1179
			if p_u_1184.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseButton1 or p_u_1184.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
				dragToggle = true
				dragStart = p_u_1184.Position
				startPos = p_u_1179.Position
				p_u_1184.Changed:Connect(function()
					-- upvalues: (ref) p_u_1184
					if p_u_1184.UserInputState == Enum.UserInputState.End then
						dragToggle = false
					end
				end)
			end
		end)
		p_u_1179.InputChanged:Connect(function(p1185)
			if p1185.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.MouseMovement or p1185.UserInputType == Enum.UserInputType.Touch then
				dragInput = p1185
			end
		end)
		game:GetService("UserInputService").InputChanged:Connect(function(p1186)
			if p1186 == dragInput and dragToggle then
				updateInput(p1186)
			end
		end)
	end
	dragify(v_u_20)
	animateIn()
